# Scan Report: Medicaid.gov —

- Issue: https://github.com/mgifford/open-scans/issues/166
- Submitted by: mgifford
- Scanned at: 2026-03-16T14:14:52.594Z
- Engines used: ALFA, AXE
- Scan duration: 17.1 minutes
- Total URLs submitted: 100
- Accepted public URLs: 100
- Rejected URLs: 0
- 🎨 **Accessibility personalization (CSS media queries):**
  - 🌙 Dark mode: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-color-scheme: dark`
  - ⚡ Reduced motion: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`
  - 🔍 High contrast: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-contrast: more`
  - 🖥️ **Forced colors:** 99 of 100 URLs (99%) support `forced-colors: active`
  - 🪟 Reduced transparency: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-reduced-transparency: reduce`
- ALFA outcomes: 85609 passed, 5893 failed, 126 cantTell, 4661 inapplicable
- axe outcomes: 69641 passed, 156 failed, 294 cantTell, 4250 inapplicable
- Equal Access outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed (0 unique, 0 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- AccessLint outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed (0 unique, 0 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- QualWeb outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed, 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- Duplicate findings caught by later scanners: 5293

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 99 page(s) - 99 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="https://data.medicaid.gov/" data-listener-attached="true">Data.Medicaid.gov</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://medicaid.gov/
- https://medicaid.gov/managed-long-term-services-supports-faqs
- https://medicaid.gov/medicaid/long-term-services-supports
- https://medicaid.gov/medicaid/long-term-services-supports/alternatives-psychiatric-residential-treatment-facilities
- https://medicaid.gov/medicaid/long-term-services-supports/balancing-long-term-services-supports

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://medicaid.gov/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="usa-button" type="submit">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-button"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a target="_self" href="/faq" aria-label="Go to Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs)" data-listener-attached="true">FAQs</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/resources-for-states/working-families-tax-cut-legislation" class="usa-button" data-listener-attached="true">Visit Page</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="usa-button"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `complementary` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.49:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-footer__contact-info margin-bottom-0">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-footer__contact-info margin-bottom-0"]`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.49:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-footer__contact-info margin-bottom-0">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-footer__contact-info margin-bottom-0"]`

- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-button"]`

- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4 class="usa-footer__primary-link">Related Sites</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4[@class="usa-footer__primary-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.49:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-footer__contact-info margin-bottom-0">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-footer__contact-info margin-bottom-0"]`

- XPath: `/th[@class="sorting_desc"]`

### https://medicaid.gov/style-guide

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="link" style="text-decoration:none;" href="#" data-listener-attached="true">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="ext-call-to-action" href="#" data-listener-attached="true">Heading three as a hyperlink</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ext-call-to-action"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="button-style">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="button-style"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="button-style hover">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="button-style hover"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="button-style visited">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="button-style visited"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R113](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r113)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<a class="link" style="text-decoration:none;" href="#" data-listener-attached="true">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="block block-medicaid-custom block-program-landing-page-blue-ribbon-block" id="block-programlandingpageblueribbonblock">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-programlandingpageblueribbonblock"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<input id="email" name="email" placeholder="e-mail here" type="email" />`
- XPath: `/input[@id="email"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)
**WCAG**: Best Practice

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4 class="usa-footer__primary-link">Related Sites</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4[@class="usa-footer__primary-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.49:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R69: Text has sufficient contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r69)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 4.03:1 which is         below the required contrast of 4.5:1

**Failure 1:**

- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-footer__contact-info margin-bottom-0"]`

- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.49:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**

- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-button"]`

- XPath: `/h4[@class="usa-footer__primary-link"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://medicaid.gov/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<aside class="grid-container" role="complementary">`
- XPath: `.landing-page-blue-ribbon > aside`

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<label style="color:#c95c68;">Arrow 20px › Use single right-pointing arrow (&amp; #8250;)</label>`
- XPath: `label:nth-child(5)`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<div style="color:#cc5127;flex:1;padding-left:20px;">Link to other.gov domains</div>`
- XPath: `.style-guide-grid-container:nth-child(3) > div > div:nth-child(2)`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<div style="color:#cc5127;flex:1;padding-left:20px;">Link to non .gov domains</div>`
- XPath: `.style-guide-grid-container:nth-child(3) > div > div:nth-child(3)`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<div style="color:#cc5127;flex:1;padding-left:20px;">`
- XPath: `.style-guide-grid-container:nth-child(5) > .row-group > div > div`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<div style="color:#cc5127;flex:1;font-size:14px;margin-left:auto;padding-left:20px;">Hyperlinked text is in default link blue and underlined, file sized indicators are not hyperlinked. if links go to other .gov domains or non .gov domains follow appending rules from above</div>`
- XPath: `.row-group:nth-child(2) > div > div:nth-child(3)`

**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested
- HTML: `<button class="button-style"><a href="" data-listener-attached="true">Button as hyper link</a></button>`

- XPath: `.hover`

- XPath: `.visited`

**Failure 4:**

- HTML: `<button class="button-style icon">`
- XPath: `.row-group:nth-child(8) > .button-row > .icon.button-style`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested
- HTML: `<button class="button-style icon">`
- XPath: `.row-group:nth-child(9) > .button-row > .icon.button-style`

- XPath: `.site-branding__logo`

### https://medicaid.gov/state-overviews/state-profiles

#### Rule: [aria-prohibited-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-prohibited-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use permitted ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div aria-disabled="true" aria-label="State Map Image. Keyboard navigating users can use dropdown to select state." id="map" style="position: relative; width: 880px; height: 502.857px; overflow: hidden; left: 0px; top: 0px;">`
- XPath: `#map`

**Impact**: moderate

- XPath: `.region-footer-first > .usa-footer__primary-content.usa-footer__primary-content--collapsible > h4`

#### Rule: [label-title-only](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/label-title-only?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Form elements should have a visible label
- HTML: `<select id="select-state" name="state" class="usa-select margin-top-0" aria-labelledby="select-state-label" aria-describedby="select-state-instructions">`
- XPath: `#select-state`
